I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
K8sattributes: Add automatic RBAC for new `service.name` resource attribute generator
The k8sattributes processor recently added support for automatic the `service.name` resource attribute:

* https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-collector-contrib/pull/39335

According to https://opentelemetry.io/docs/specs/semconv/non-normative/k8s-attributes/#how-servicename-should-be-calculated, the `service.name` is extract from the first of these attributes:

* pod.annotation[resource.opentelemetry.io/service.name]
* pod.label[app.kubernetes.io/instance]
* pod.label[app.kubernetes.io/name]
* k8s.deployment.name
* k8s.replicaset.name
* k8s.statefulset.name
* k8s.daemonset.name
* k8s.cronjob.name
* k8s.job.name
* k8s.pod.name
* k8s.container.name

This means that, if k8sprocessor has been configured with `service.name`, https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-operator/blob/149d03c1b291be5bd3dd116783f443d4fc63c6fb/internal/components/processors/k8sattribute.go#L34 should automatically add RBAC for `replicasets` (to access `k8s.deployment.name`).

</pr_description>

    14	type FieldExtractConfig struct {
    15	        TagName  string `mapstructure:"tag_name"`
    16	        Key      string `mapstructure:"key"`
    17	        KeyRegex string `mapstructure:"key_regex"`
    18	        Regex    string `mapstructure:"regex"`
    19	        From     string `mapstructure:"from"`
    20	}
    21	
    22	type Extract struct {
    23	        Metadata    []string             `mapstructure:"metadata"`
    24	        Labels      []FieldExtractConfig `mapstructure:"labels"`
    25	        Annotations []FieldExtractConfig `mapstructure:"annotations"`
    26	}
    27	
    28	// K8sAttributeConfig is a minimal struct needed for parsing a valid k8sattribute processor configuration
    29	// This only contains the fields necessary for parsing, other fields can be added in the future.
    30	type K8sAttributeConfig struct {
    31	        Extract Extract `mapstructure:"extract"`
    32	}
    33	
    34	func GenerateK8SAttrRbacRules(_ logr.Logger, config K8sAttributeConfig) ([]rbacv1.PolicyRule, error) {
    35	        // These policies need to be added always
    36	        var prs = []rbacv1.PolicyRule{
    37	                {
    38	                        APIGroups: []string{""},
    39	                        Resources: []string{"pods", "namespaces"},
    40	                        Verbs:     []string{"get", "watch", "list"},
    41	                },
    42	        }
    43	
    44	        replicasetPolicy := rbacv1.PolicyRule{
    45	                APIGroups: []string{"apps"},
    46	                Resources: []string{"replicasets"},
    47	                Verbs:     []string{"get", "watch", "list"},
    48	        }
    49	
    50	        if len(config.Extract.Metadata) == 0 {
    51	                prs = append(prs, replicasetPolicy)
    52	        }
    53	        addedReplicasetPolicy := false
    54	        for _, m := range config.Extract.Metadata {
    55	                metadataField := fmt.Sprint(m)
    56	                if (metadataField == "k8s.deployment.uid" || metadataField == "k8s.deployment.name") && !addedReplicasetPolicy {
    57	                        prs = append(prs, replicasetPolicy)
    58	                        addedReplicasetPolicy = true
    59	                } else if strings.Contains(metadataField, "k8s.node") {
    60	                        prs = append(prs,
    61	                                rbacv1.PolicyRule{
    62	                                        APIGroups: []string{""},
    63	                                        Resources: []string{"nodes"},
    64	                                        Verbs:     []string{"get", "watch", "list"},
    65	                                },
    66	                        )
    67	                }
    68	        }
    69	        return prs, nil
    70	}

   399	// chooseServiceName returns the service name to be used in the instrumentation.
   400	// See https://github.com/open-telemetry/semantic-conventions/blob/main/docs/non-normative/k8s-attributes.md#how-servicename-should-be-calculated
   401	func chooseServiceName(pod corev1.Pod, useLabelsForResourceAttributes bool, resources map[string]string, index int) string {
   402	        if name := chooseLabelOrAnnotation(pod, useLabelsForResourceAttributes, semconv.ServiceNameKey, constants.LabelAppName); name != "" {
   403	                return name
   404	        }
   405	        if name := resources[string(semconv.K8SDeploymentNameKey)]; name != "" {
   406	                return name
   407	        }
   408	        if name := resources[string(semconv.K8SReplicaSetNameKey)]; name != "" {
   409	                return name
   410	        }
   411	        if name := resources[string(semconv.K8SStatefulSetNameKey)]; name != "" {
   412	                return name
   413	        }
   414	        if name := resources[string(semconv.K8SDaemonSetNameKey)]; name != "" {
   415	                return name
   416	        }
   417	        if name := resources[string(semconv.K8SCronJobNameKey)]; name != "" {
   418	                return name
   419	        }
   420	        if name := resources[string(semconv.K8SJobNameKey)]; name != "" {
   421	                return name
   422	        }
   423	        if name := resources[string(semconv.K8SPodNameKey)]; name != "" {
   424	                return name
   425	        }
   426	        return pod.Spec.Containers[index].Name
   427	}
   428	
   429	// chooseLabelOrAnnotation returns the value of the label or annotation with the given key.
   430	// The precedence is as follows:
   431	// 1. annotation with key resource.opentelemetry.io/<resource>.
   432	// 2. label with key labelKey.
   433	func chooseLabelOrAnnotation(pod corev1.Pod, useLabelsForResourceAttributes bool, resource attribute.Key, labelKeys []string) string {
   434	        if v := pod.GetAnnotations()[(constants.ResourceAttributeAnnotationPrefix + string(resource))]; v != "" {
   435	                return v
   436	        }
   437	        if useLabelsForResourceAttributes {
   438	                for _, labelKey := range labelKeys {
   439	                        if v := pod.GetLabels()[labelKey]; v != "" {
   440	                                return v
   441	                        }
   442	                }
   443	        }
   444	        return ""
   445	}

    30	type K8sAttributeConfig struct {
    31	        Extract Extract `mapstructure:"extract"`
    32	}
    33	
    34	func GenerateK8SAttrRbacRules(_ logr.Logger, config K8sAttributeConfig) ([]rbacv1.PolicyRule, error) {
    35	        // These policies need to be added always
    36	        var prs = []rbacv1.PolicyRule{
    37	                {
    38	                        APIGroups: []string{""},
    39	                        Resources: []string{"pods", "namespaces"},
    40	                        Verbs:     []string{"get", "watch", "list"},
    41	                },
    42	        }
    43	
    44	        replicasetPolicy := rbacv1.PolicyRule{
    45	                APIGroups: []string{"apps"},
    46	                Resources: []string{"replicasets"},
    47	                Verbs:     []string{"get", "watch", "list"},
    48	        }
    49	
    50	        if len(config.Extract.Metadata) == 0 {
    51	                prs = append(prs, replicasetPolicy)
    52	        }
    53	        addedReplicasetPolicy := false
    54	        for _, m := range config.Extract.Metadata {
    55	                metadataField := fmt.Sprint(m)
    56	                if (metadataField == "k8s.deployment.uid" || metadataField == "k8s.deployment.name") && !addedReplicasetPolicy {
    57	                        prs = append(prs, replicasetPolicy)
    58	                        addedReplicasetPolicy = true
    59	                } else if strings.Contains(metadataField, "k8s.node") {
    60	                        prs = append(prs,
    61	                                rbacv1.PolicyRule{
    62	                                        APIGroups: []string{""},
    63	                                        Resources: []string{"nodes"},
    64	                                        Verbs:     []string{"get", "watch", "list"},
    65	                                },
    66	                        )
    67	                }
    68	        }
    69	        return prs, nil
    70	}

     1	// Copyright The OpenTelemetry Authors
     2	// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
     3	
     4	package processors
     5	
     6	import "github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-operator/internal/components"
     7	
     8	// registry holds a record of all known receiver parsers.
     9	var registry = make(map[string]components.Parser)
    10	
    11	// Register adds a new parser builder to the list of known builders.
    12	func Register(name string, p components.Parser) {
    13	        registry[name] = p
    14	}
    15	
    16	// IsRegistered checks whether a parser is registered with the given name.
    17	func IsRegistered(name string) bool {
    18	        _, ok := registry[components.ComponentType(name)]
    19	        return ok
    20	}
    21	
    22	// ProcessorFor returns a parser builder for the given exporter name.
    23	func ProcessorFor(name string) components.Parser {
    24	        if parser, ok := registry[components.ComponentType(name)]; ok {
    25	                return parser
    26	        }
    27	        return components.NewBuilder[any]().WithName(name).MustBuild()
    28	}
    29	
    30	var componentParsers = []components.Parser{
    31	        components.NewBuilder[K8sAttributeConfig]().WithName("k8sattributes").WithRbacGen(GenerateK8SAttrRbacRules).MustBuild(),
    32	        components.NewBuilder[ResourceDetectionConfig]().WithName("resourcedetection").WithRbacGen(GenerateResourceDetectionRbacRules).MustBuild(),
    33	}
    34	
    35	func init() {
    36	        for _, parser := range componentParsers {
    37	                Register(parser.ParserType(), parser)
    38	        }
    39	}
    40

Based on my analysis, I understand the issue now. The PR description states that when the k8sattributes processor is configured to extract the `service.name` attribute automatically, it needs RBAC permissions to access `replicasets` to retrieve the `k8s.deployment.name`.

Looking at the code in `/testbed/internal/components/processors/k8sattribute.go`, the current logic only adds the replicaset policy when:
1. The metadata list is empty (lines 50-52), OR
2. When specific metadata fields (`k8s.deployment.uid` or `k8s.deployment.name`) are explicitly configured (lines 54-59).

However, according to the PR description, when `service.name` is configured (which will use `k8s.deployment.name` as one of the fallback options), the RBAC for replicasets should also be added automatically.

str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_k8sattribute_rbac.go --file_text 'package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"log"

	"github.com/go-logr/logr"
	rbacv1 "k8s.io/api/rbac/v1"
	"github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-operator/internal/components/processors"
)

func main() {
	logger := logr.Discard()
	
	// Test case 1: Empty config (should add replicasets)
fmt.Println("Test 1: Empty metadata")
	config1 := processors.K8sAttributeConfig{
		Extract: processors.Extract{
			Metadata: []string{},
		},
	}
	rules1, err := processors.GenerateK8SAttrRbacRules(logger, config1)
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatal(err)
	}
	printRules(rules1)
	
	// Test case 2: Config with deployment.name (should add replicasets)
fmt.Println("\nTest 2: Metadata contains k8s.deployment.name")
	config2 := processors.K8sAttributeConfig{
		Extract: processors.Extract{
			Metadata: []string{"k8s.deployment.name"},
		},
	}
	rules2, err := processors.GenerateK8SAttrRbacRules(logger, config2)
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatal(err)
	}
	printRules(rules2)

	// Test case 3: Config with service.name (should add replicasets)
	fmt.Println("\nTest 3: Metadata contains service.name")
	config3 := processors.K8sAttributeConfig{
		Extract: processors.Extract{
			Metadata: []string{"service.name"},
		},
	}
	rules3, err := processors.GenerateK8SAttrRbacRules(logger, config3)
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatal(err)
	}
	printRules(rules3)
}

func printRules(rules []rbacv1.PolicyRule) {
	for i, rule := range rules {
		fmt.Printf("Rule %d: APIGroups=%v, Resources=%v, Verbs=%v\n", i+1, rule.APIGroups, rule.Resources, rule.Verbs)
	}
}'

Now I understand the issue. The current code only adds RBAC rules for `replicasets` when `k8s.deployment.uid` or `k8s.deployment.name` are in the metadata. However, based on the PR description, when the k8sattributes processor is configured with automatic `service.name` extraction, it should also add RBAC rules for `replicasets` since `service.name` can be derived from `k8s.deployment.name` (among other sources).

The PR description indicates that if k8sprocessor has been configured with `service.name`, it should automatically add RBAC for `replicasets` to access `k8s.deployment.name`.

Let me modify the code to handle this case:

                        prs = append(prs, replicasetPolicy)
                        addedReplicasetPolicy = true
                } else if strings.Contains(metadataField, "k8s.node") {

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_k8sattribute_comprehensive.go --file_text 'package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"log"

	"github.com/go-logr/logr"
	rbacv1 "k8s.io/api/rbac/v1"
	"github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-operator/internal/components/processors"
)

func main() {
	logger := logr.Discard()
	
	testCases := []struct {
		name   string
		config processors.K8sAttributeConfig
		expectReplicaset bool
	}{
		{
			name: "Empty metadata (should add replicasets)",
			config: processors.K8sAttributeConfig{
				Extract: processors.Extract{
					Metadata: []string{},
				},
			},
			expectReplicaset: true,
		},
		{
			name: "k8s.deployment.name (should add replicasets)",
			config: processors.K8sAttributeConfig{
				Extract: processors.Extract{
					Metadata: []string{"k8s.deployment.name"},
				},
			},
			expectReplicaset: true,
		},
		{
			name: "k8s.deployment.uid (should add replicasets)",
			config: processors.K8sAttributeConfig{
				Extract: processors.Extract{
					Metadata: []string{"k8s.deployment.uid"},
				},
			},
			expectReplicaset: true,
		},
		{
			name: "service.name (should add replicasets)",
			config: processors.K8sAttributeConfig{
				Extract: processors.Extract{
					Metadata: []string{"service.name"},
				},
			},
			expectReplicaset: true,
		},
		{
			name: "service.name with other metadata (should add replicasets)",
			config: processors.K8sAttributeConfig{
				Extract: processors.Extract{
					Metadata: []string{"service.name", "k8s.pod.name"},
				},
			},
			expectReplicaset: true,
		},
		{
			name: "k8s.node.name (should not add replicasets)",
			config: processors.K8sAttributeConfig{
				Extract: processors.Extract{
					Metadata: []string{"k8s.node.name"},
				},
			},
			expectReplicaset: false,
		},
		{
			name: "Other metadata (should not add replicasets)",
			config: processors.K8sAttributeConfig{
				Extract: processors.Extract{
					Metadata: []string{"k8s.pod.name"},
				},
			},
			expectReplicaset: false,
		},
	}

	allPassed := true
	for _, tc := range testCases {
		rules, err := processors.GenerateK8SAttrRbacRules(logger, tc.config)
		if err != nil {
			log.Printf("Test %s failed with error: %v", tc.name, err)
			allPassed = false
			continue
		}

		hasReplicaset := false
		for _, rule := range rules {
			for _, resource := range rule.Resources {
				if resource == "replicasets" {
					hasReplicaset = true
					break
				}
			}
		}

		if hasReplicaset != tc.expectReplicaset {
			log.Printf("Test %s failed: expected replicaset=%v, got replicaset=%v", tc.name, tc.expectReplicaset, hasReplicaset)
			allPassed = false
			printRules(rules)
		} else {
			fmt.Printf("✓ %s\n", tc.name)
		}
	}

	if allPassed {
		fmt.Println("\nAll tests passed!")
	} else {
		fmt.Println("\nSome tests failed!")
	}
}

func printRules(rules []rbacv1.PolicyRule) {
	for i, rule := range rules {
		fmt.Printf("  Rule %d: APIGroups=%v, Resources=%v, Verbs=%v\n", i+1, rule.APIGroups, rule.Resources, rule.Verbs)
	}
}'

import (
	"fmt"

	"github.com/go-logr/logr"
	"github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-operator/internal/components/processors"
)

func main() {
	logger := logr.Discard()

	// Test 1: service.name should add replicasets RBAC
	config1 := processors.K8sAttributeConfig{
		Extract: processors.Extract{
			Metadata: []string{"service.name"},
		},
	}
	rules1, _ := processors.GenerateK8SAttrRbacRules(logger, config1)
	
	hasReplicasets := false
	for _, rule := range rules1 {
		for _, resource := range rule.Resources {
			if resource == "replicasets" {
				hasReplicasets = true
			}
		}
	}

	if hasReplicasets {
		fmt.Println("✓ Test 1 passed: service.name correctly adds replicasets RBAC")
	} else {
		fmt.Println("✗ Test 1 failed: service.name does not add replicasets RBAC")
	}

	// Test 2: Verify other metadata still works
	config2 := processors.K8sAttributeConfig{
		Extract: processors.Extract{
			Metadata: []string{"k8s.deployment.name"},
		},
	}
	rules2, _ := processors.GenerateK8SAttrRbacRules(logger, config2)
	
	hasReplicasets2 := false
	for _, rule := range rules2 {
		for _, resource := range rule.Resources {
			if resource == "replicasets" {
				hasReplicasets2 = true
			}
		}
	}

	if hasReplicasets2 {
		fmt.Println("✓ Test 2 passed: k8s.deployment.name still adds replicasets RBAC")
	} else {
		fmt.Println("✗ Test 2 failed: k8s.deployment.name does not add replicasets RBAC")
	}

	// Test 3: service.name with other metadata
	config3 := processors.K8sAttributeConfig{
		Extract: processors.Extract{
			Metadata: []string{"service.name", "k8s.pod.name"},
		},
	}
	rules3, _ := processors.GenerateK8SAttrRbacRules(logger, config3)
	
	hasReplicasets3 := false
	for _, rule := range rules3 {
		for _, resource := range rule.Resources {
			if resource == "replicasets" {
				hasReplicasets3 = true
			}
		}
	}

	if hasReplicasets3 {
		fmt.Println("✓ Test 3 passed: service.name with other metadata correctly adds replicasets RBAC")
	} else {
		fmt.Println("✗ Test 3 failed: service.name with other metadata does not add replicasets RBAC")
	}

	// Test 4: Non-deployment related metadata should not add replicasets
	config4 := processors.K8sAttributeConfig{
		Extract: processors.Extract{
			Metadata: []string{"k8s.pod.name"},
		},
	}
	rules4, _ := processors.GenerateK8SAttrRbacRules(logger, config4)
	
	hasReplicasets4 := false
	for _, rule := range rules4 {
		for _, resource := range rule.Resources {
			if resource == "replicasets" {
				hasReplicasets4 = true
			}
		}
	}

	if !hasReplicasets4 {
		fmt.Println("✓ Test 4 passed: Non-deployment metadata correctly does not add replicasets RBAC")
	} else {
		fmt.Println("✗ Test 4 failed: Non-deployment metadata incorrectly adds replicasets RBAC")
	}

	fmt.Println("\nAll tests completed!")
}'
